\doxysubsection{Descripción detallada}
\begin{DoxyVerb}Represents something that may be installed later on, may have information
about where to fetch the relevant requirement and also contains logic for
installing the said requirement.
\end{DoxyVerb}

 None pip.\+\_\+internal.\+req.\+req\+\_\+install.\+Install\+Requirement.\+archive (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{str \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} None}]{build\+\_\+dir}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Saves archive to provided build_dir.

Used for saving downloaded VCS requirements as part of `pip download`.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Ensure that a source_dir is set.

This will create a temporary build dir if the name of the requirement
isn't known yet.

:param parent_dir: The ideal pip parent_dir for the source_dir.
    Generally src_dir for editables and build_dir for sdists.
:return: self.source_dir
\end{DoxyVerb}

\Hypertarget{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1req_1_1req__install_1_1_install_requirement_acf56120e2e7c5046433147b7b496f74a}\index{pip.\_internal.req.req\_install.InstallRequirement@{pip.\_internal.req.req\_install.InstallRequirement}!hashes@{hashes}}
\index{hashes@{hashes}!pip.\_internal.req.req\_install.InstallRequirement@{pip.\_internal.req.req\_install.InstallRequirement}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hashes()}{hashes()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1req_1_1req__install_1_1_install_requirement_acf56120e2e7c5046433147b7b496f74a} 
 \mbox{\hyperlink{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1utils_1_1hashes_1_1_hashes}{Hashes}} pip.\+\_\+internal.\+req.\+req\+\_\+install.\+Install\+Requirement.\+hashes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{bool }]{trust\+\_\+internet}{ = {\ttfamily True}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Return a hash-comparer that considers my option- and URL-based
hashes to be known-good.

Hashes in URLs--ones embedded in the requirements file, not ones
downloaded from an index server--are almost peers with ones from
flags. They satisfy --require-hashes (whether it was implicitly or
explicitly activated) but do not activate it. md5 and sha224 are not
allowed in flags, which should nudge people toward good algos. We
always OR all hashes together, even ones from URLs.

:param trust_internet: Whether to trust URL-based (#md5=...) hashes
    downloaded from the internet, as by populate_link()
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definición en la línea \mbox{\hyperlink{micro__gestion__objetos_2venv_2_lib_2site-packages_2pip_2__internal_2req_2req__install_8py_source_l00305}{305}} del archivo \mbox{\hyperlink{micro__gestion__objetos_2venv_2_lib_2site-packages_2pip_2__internal_2req_2req__install_8py_source}{req\+\_\+install.\+py}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1req_1_1req__install_1_1_install_requirement_acf56120e2e7c5046433147b7b496f74a} 
 \mbox{\hyperlink{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1utils_1_1hashes_1_1_hashes}{Hashes}} pip.\+\_\+internal.\+req.\+req\+\_\+install.\+Install\+Requirement.\+hashes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{bool }]{trust\+\_\+internet}{ = {\ttfamily True}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

follow the PEP 517 or legacy (setup.py) code path.

 None pip.\+\_\+internal.\+req.\+req\+\_\+install.\+Install\+Requirement.\+prepare\+\_\+metadata (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Ensure that project metadata is available.

Under PEP 517 and PEP 660, call the backend hook to prepare the metadata.
Under legacy processing, call setup.py egg-info.
\end{DoxyVerb}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1req_1_1req__install_1_1_install_requirement_a0cddcae8523c5e6a484f0213c09caea8} 
 None pip.\+\_\+internal.\+req.\+req\+\_\+install.\+Install\+Requirement.\+prepare\+\_\+metadata (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Ensure that project metadata is available.

Under PEP 517 and PEP 660, call the backend hook to prepare the metadata.
Under legacy processing, call setup.py egg-info.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\index{uninstall@{uninstall}!pip.\_internal.req.req\_install.InstallRequirement@{pip.\_internal.req.req\_install.InstallRequirement}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{uninstall()}{uninstall()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1req_1_1req__install_1_1_install_requirement_aa38d1dde88424b2494ac7eabf84ebff1} 
 \mbox{\hyperlink{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1req_1_1req__uninstall_1_1_uninstall_path_set}{Uninstall\+Path\+Set}} \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} None pip.\+\_\+internal.\+req.\+req\+\_\+install.\+Install\+Requirement.\+uninstall (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{bool }]{auto\+\_\+confirm}{ = {\ttfamily False}, }\item[{bool }]{verbose}{ = {\ttfamily False}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Uninstall the distribution currently satisfying this requirement.

Prompts before removing or modifying files unless
``auto_confirm`` is True.

Refuses to delete or modify files outside of ``sys.prefix`` -
thus uninstallation within a virtual environment can only
modify that virtual environment, even if the virtualenv is
linked to global site-packages.
\end{DoxyVerb}
